Privilege_ManaCost = {
	[[adm_power]
	add_adm_power = -$adm_power$
	]
	[[dip_power]add_dip_power = -$dip_power$
	]
	[[mil_power]add_mil_power = -$mil_power$
	]
}


Privilege_NOProcessingLower = {
	if = {
   		limit = {
   			Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=1 }
   		}
		Privilege_NOProcessing0LowerReqs = yes
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Privilege_NOProcessing0Lower_description
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		if = {
			limit = {
				Privilege_NOProcessing0CanLower = yes
			}
			Privilege_NOProcessing0Lower = yes
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = { Privilege_NOProcessing0Lower = yes } # dont actually do it
			[[event]
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = $event$ } }
			]
		}
   	}
 
	else_if = {
   		limit = {
   			Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 }
   		}
		Privilege_NOProcessing1LowerReqs = yes
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Privilege_NOProcessing1Lower_description
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		if = {
			limit = {
				Privilege_NOProcessing1CanLower = yes
			}
			Privilege_NOProcessing1Lower = yes
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = { Privilege_NOProcessing1Lower = yes } # dont actually do it
			[[event]
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = $event$ } }
			]
		}
   	}
}

	}

   		}

		custom_tooltip = Privilege_NOServiceE0Lower_description
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					Privilege_NOServiceE0CanLower = yes
					NOT = { always = $costs$ }
				}
			}
			Privilege_NOServiceE0Lower = { costs = $costs$ }
		}

			tooltip = { Privilege_NOServiceE0Lower = yes } # dont actually do it

   		limit = {
   			Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BGEmbargo Lvl=1 }
   		}
		Privilege_BGEmbargo0LowerReqs = yes
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Privilege_BGEmbargo0Lower_description
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		if = {
			limit = {
				Privilege_BGEmbargo0CanLower = yes
			}
			Privilege_BGEmbargo0Lower = yes
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = { Privilege_BGEmbargo0Lower = yes } # dont actually do it
			[[event]hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = $event$ } }]
		}
   	}

Privilege_BURotateLower = {
	if = {
   		limit = {
   			Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BURotate Lvl=1 }
   		}
		Privilege_BURotate0LowerReqs = yes
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Privilege_BURotate0Lower_description
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		if = {
			limit = {
				Privilege_BURotate0CanLower = yes
			}
			Privilege_BURotate0Lower = yes
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = { Privilege_BURotate0Lower = yes } # dont actually do it
			[[event]hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = $event$ } }]
		}
   	}
}

Privilege_BURotateRaise = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BURotate Lvl=0 }
		}
		Privilege_BURotate1RaiseReqs = yes
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Privilege_BURotate1Raise_description
		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		if = {
			limit = {
				Privilege_BURotate1CanRaise = yes
			}
			Privilege_BURotate1Raise = yes
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = { Privilege_BURotate1Raise = yes } # dont actually do it
			[[event]hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = $event$ } }]
		}
	}
}
